Immediately, over 300 students were gathered, stood solemnly on the playground, and listened to the lecture. Lin said, in brief, "Today, I came to your school for inspection. I am very grateful that you have requested a lecture on the New Life Movement. It would be a long discussion, but to save valuable time, I will simply say that it is about incorporating neatness, simplicity, cleanliness, and plainness into daily life, using it as a standard for daily discipline in schools, making it a daily habit in families, and treating propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame as the creed of young students. If you can implement it in everything you do, even if you cannot achieve it completely, the results will be considerable."

Afternoon Tea Party at the Municipal Government

Because the four inspectors had completed their inspection in Shanghai, the Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association specially convened a tea party at the Municipal Government at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon, gathering principals and discipline directors of major middle schools and universities in Shanghai, as well as heads of various agencies and leaders from various sectors. More than 200 people attended, including Mayor Wu, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau Wu, Director of the Education Bureau Pan, Director of the Land Bureau Jin, Director of the Public Works Bureau Xu, as well as Lu Jingshi, Zhang Shouyong, Li Dachao, Ou Yuanhuai, Shen Junru, Lin Keting, Yan Zhenyu, and Yang Jingyi. Mayor Wu, Director Pan, and Director Wu presided over the meeting. Director Pan first gave a welcome speech, hoping that the four inspectors of the New Life Movement would offer detailed criticisms of the New Life Movement in Shanghai to serve as a guide.

Mr. Xu Speaks on the New Life Movement

Then, Xu Qingyu, leader of the inspection group, gave a speech, saying, in brief, "I was ordered to come to Shanghai to inspect the New Life Movement, and today it has been completed. The construction of the city center area and the promotion of the New Life Movement in Shanghai have made great progress due to the leadership of responsible party and government personnel and leaders from various sectors. The increase in administrative efficiency and the enthusiasm of the service corps are indeed good phenomena. Moreover, the youth service corps stand at attention and salute when mentioning Premier Sun and Chairman Chiang, which shows the enthusiasm of these young people in supporting the leaders, which makes me even more motivated. However, during this inspection, there are still one or two minor shortcomings, but I deeply believe that the sincerity of the Shanghai municipal authorities and leaders from various sectors in promoting the New Life Movement will lead to unlimited progress in the future. However, what we must pay attention to is the method of promoting the New Life Movement. I believe that the promotion of the New Life Movement should be the joint responsibility of schools and families. If families and schools can implement the New Life Movement, then children and students will inevitably be influenced. We should clearly understand that the success or failure of the New Life Movement is of great importance to the country and the nation. You are leaders from all walks of life in Shanghai. If you can effectively promote the New Life Movement, not only will the New Life Movement in Shanghai make progress, but the whole country will also be inspired."

Speeches by Leaders from Various Sectors

Next, Ou Yuanhuai gave a speech, saying, in brief, "School education is for cultivating knowledge and character, and the purpose of the New Life Movement is also to cultivate the knowledge of being a person. In other words, it is to cultivate a citizen with a sound personality." Then, Zhang Shouyong gave a speech, saying, in brief, "School textbooks are currently unable to be unified, and the inherent Chinese morality cannot be fully incorporated. In the future, when compiling textbooks, I hope that more of the New Life Movement guidelines will be adopted." Later, Shen Junru gave a speech, saying that the promotion of the New Life Movement should start with oneself, with one's position, with small things, with the family, and with the entire society, so that there will be progress.

Mayor and Bureau Directors Respond

Finally, Mayor Wu gave a response, saying, in brief, "The New Life Movement inspection tour group has completed its inspection in Shanghai, and it should have a judgment on the New Life Movement in Shanghai. Is there still anything incomplete in the New Life Movement, or anything that cannot be implemented? The inspectors come from Nanchang, the birthplace of the New Life Movement, and have stayed in Shanghai for five days. They should have a judgment on the New Life Movement in Shanghai. We sincerely hope that Director Xu will give us guidance so that we can gain a new direction in promoting the New Life Movement. We believe that when the four inspectors come to Shanghai again for inspection, the New Life Movement in Shanghai will make progress. The New Life Movement is a movement for building the country and revitalizing the nation. If the New Life Movement can succeed, then we can build the country and revitalize the nation. We know that the hope of a family lies in the talent of its children, and the strength of a country and nation depends on the revitalization of the national spirit. We also know that the interpretation of phenomena is a total expression of a nation's life. By observing this total expression of a nation's life, we can determine the strength or weakness of this nation. We hope that those who implement the New Life Movement can strive to promote it at all times, day by day, month by month, year by year, and throughout their lives, following the outline of the New Life Movement. Only then can the New Life Movement be popularized." Finally, Director Wu Xingya gave a thank-you speech, in addition to thanking the inspectors and guests for their instructions, he also added a detailed explanation of the four characters of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame, and encouraged the education sector to do its best to promote the New Life Movement.

Mr. Xu Talks about His Impressions of the Inspection

Xu Qingyu, leader of the New Life Movement Association inspection tour group, and his party of four, came to Shanghai for a five-day inspection and had an excellent impression, especially with high hopes for the Youth Service Corps organized by the New Life Movement Association. Yesterday, Mr. Xu expressed his impressions of the inspection to a reporter from the Kuomintang News Agency, saying, "Since the implementation of the New Life Movement in Shanghai, it has aroused the attention of people from all walks of life. Although its effectiveness has not been fully demonstrated, it is probably because the environment is mixed with Chinese and foreigners, and the environment is harsh, which cannot be achieved in a short period of time. We have had quite a few impressions from our recent inspections, which can be told to people from all walks of life in Shanghai: (1) The local party, government, and military authorities are united, and public officials can use scientific methods in handling affairs, such as the storage of files in various bureaus of the municipal government and the organization of social statistical surveys, all of which are well-organized and more advanced than the inland agencies. (2) The cleanliness and tidiness of the internal affairs of agencies and schools have been achieved, but many college students wear Western clothes. In the future, they should all be changed to uniforms and strive for simplicity. A small number of students smoke, and the school authorities should strictly ban them. (3) There are more than 30,000 shanty towns in the four suburbs near Shanghai. Due to the limited financial resources of the municipal government, it is impossible to rebuild all of them into affordable housing. There are quite a few wealthy people in the city who are not lacking in compassion. They should be motivated to donate money and transform the shanty towns, so that hundreds of thousands of poor people who are exposed to the elements can have a place to live. Shanghai is a major commercial port in East Asia. If the shanty towns are not transformed, it will not only hinder the appearance but also endanger the lives and health of the poor and the public health of the society. (4) The daily life of the middle class and above is too extravagant. At a time when the countryside is collapsing and starving people are everywhere, we must practice thrift and promote domestic products. We express our sympathy for the indigenous cloth movement promoted by Mr. Shi Hengqing and Mr. Tai Shuangqiu. Guanzi said, 'The number of extravagant expenses cannot be used in a country with dangerous straits.' This sentence can be used as a motto for us. (5) The Youth Service Corps under the leadership of the New Life Movement Promotion Association is disciplined and energetic, and can be the basic team for promoting the New Life Movement. If it can be sustained, it will be very effective. In short, the New Life Movement has a major mission, and its purpose is to seek the revitalization of the nation. To improve the living habits of a group of people cannot be achieved in a month. We must adhere to the spirit of perseverance, persist to the end, and carry it through to the end. The most feared thing is to start with a bang and end with a whimper, perfunctory and negligent. Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame are the 'spiritual national defense' of the nation, which is more important than material construction. Shanghai is a gathering place for talents from all over the country. Intellectuals should be mobilized to promote the New Life Movement and save the country and survive. This is a crucial moment. It is not allowed to stand by and do nothing. Empty talk is enough to mislead the country. The key is to practice what you preach. If Shanghai implements it effectively, it will not be difficult to apply it to the whole country. There have been very few labor disputes in Shanghai recently, and the society is stable, which shows that Mayor Wu is leading effectively, and it also shows the public-mindedness of the industrial and commercial groups. Qingyu would like to express his gratitude to the local authorities and the industrial and commercial groups on behalf of the general association."

Departed for Hangzhou Yesterday Afternoon

Xu Qingyu, Zhang Yuchong, Lin Xueyan, and Yu Zhongqi, the four members of the New Life Movement Association inspection tour group, arrived in Shanghai on the evening of the 17th of this month and began inspecting the New Life Movement in various parts of Shanghai the next day. By yesterday, it had been five days. Details of the inspection have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. The group was scheduled to inspect in Shanghai for five days. Leader Xu received a telegram from Chairman Huang of the Zhejiang Provincial Government yesterday, welcoming them. Therefore, the two railway bureaus specially prepared a car, and at 6:50 PM yesterday evening, they took the Shanghai-Zhejiang express train to Hangzhou. Those who saw them off at the station included the mayor and directors of various bureaus, as well as representatives from the municipal party headquarters, all staff members of the New Life Movement Association, representatives from various sectors, and directors of the two railway bureaus. The atmosphere at the North Station was tense for a while. When Mr. Xu was about to leave, he told a reporter from the Kuomintang News Agency, "We plan to inspect in Hangzhou for three days, then go to Ningbo for a brief memorial service. If there is time, we will inspect the area along the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway and then go to Fuzhou. However, I (Xu himself) received a telegram from the Wuchang headquarters, so whether I will go to Fuzhou has not been decided, but the three inspectors Zhang, Lin, and Yu will go according to the planned itinerary."

Hunan Province's Million-Dollar Loan: Contract to be Signed Today 118

Shanghai to Lend an Additional 150,000 Yuan, Agricultural and Commercial Bank to Lend 180,000 Yuan; Contracts for Both Banks Signed Yesterday, with Dates Set for Payment

According to the Xinxin News Agency, the Hunan Provincial Construction Public Bond secured loan from the Shanghai banking community is generally complete as a result of continuous negotiations by Zhang Kailian, Director of the Department of Finance of Hunan Province, and Yu Jichuan, Director of the Department of Construction. In addition to the 1 million yuan borrowed by the Central, China, and Communications Banks, which is scheduled to be signed today, Shanghai will borrow an additional 150,000 yuan, and the Agricultural and Commercial Bank will borrow 180,000 yuan, both of which have been formally signed with dates set for payment. The following is a breakdown of the information learned by the Xinxin News Agency reporter:

Agreement Reached by Three Banks

After the 1 million yuan borrowed by the Central, China, and Communications Banks was agreed upon the previous day, a draft contract was negotiated at 1:00 PM yesterday in the office of the Director of the Business Bureau of the Central Bank. Those who attended included Xi Deyi from the Central Bank, Chen Muhua from China Bank, Zhang Peishen from the Communications Bank, Zhang Kailian from the Hunan Department of Finance, and Yu Jichuan from the Department of Construction. Mr. Yu read the drafted contract clause by clause, and the representatives of each bank revised it. By 2:15 PM, the draft contract was fully agreed upon and could have been signed on the same day. However, because the contract had to be approved by the board meeting of the Central Bank held at 4:00 PM yesterday afternoon, it was specially postponed to today for signing. The contract stipulates that the payment will be made in three installments: (1) 500,000 yuan will be paid on the 31st of this month; (2) 250,000 yuan will be paid on April 15th; (3) 250,000 yuan will be paid on June 15th. The interest rate is 8%, and the loan will be repaid in two years.

Signing by Two Banks

Yesterday, according to Zhang and Yu, the two directors, told the Xinxin News Agency reporter that the Hunan Provincial Government believes that the three major highways in Hunan Province are related to the suppression of bandits and military transportation, but the road surface is wide and long, the project is huge, and a lot of money is needed. Now, it will use a public bond with a face value of 3 million yuan to borrow 180,000 yuan from the Agricultural and Commercial Bank. The bank is enthusiastic to help, so it has formally signed the contract and set the end of this month to start payment. This loan is entirely used for the construction of the Pingjiang to Tongcheng section of the Hunan-Hubei trunk line. The section is more than 100 li long and has already started construction. It is limited to be completed and opened to traffic within three months. In addition, the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank independently borrowed 150,000 yuan, and officially signed a loan contract in the bank’s second floor at 3:00 pm yesterday. The public bond with a face value of 250,000 was mortgaged at 60% discount, and the money was paid in two installments: the first installment of 100,000 yuan was paid at the end of April this year, and the second installment of 50,000 yuan was paid at the end of June. The interest rate is 8%, and the loan is used to build the Hunan-Guizhou Highway.

Scheduled to Go to Hankou

The province's planned program was originally intended to borrow more than 2 million yuan to cope with the situation, and 1.33 million yuan has been successfully borrowed. It has not yet reached the original amount. It is now decided to continue to mortgage 800,000 yuan to the Jin Cheng, Ju Xing Cheng, China Agricultural and Industrial, China Industrial, and Continental banks. After continuous negotiations in Shanghai, each bank has agreed to help. However, the head offices of the above banks are all in the Hankou area, so Zhang and Yu, the two directors, are scheduled to leave Shanghai for Nanjing on the 25th to liaise with the Economic Committee, and then proceed from Nanjing to Hankou to continue negotiations. Once completed, they will return to Hunan to report.

Four Exchanges Submit Request to the Ministry of Finance Again: Please Postpone the Transaction Tax 120

Various Industries Are Currently in Decline and Cannot Afford It; Permission Granted to Postpone the Tax Until Business Conditions Improve in the Future

The five exchanges in Shanghai, due to the Ministry of Finance's scheduled collection of transaction taxes, collectively appealed to the central authorities, requesting a postponement. Later, the central government, considering that the Securities Exchange was purely an agency for trading national bonds, allowed it to be exempt from taxation within a possible scope. However, the remaining exchanges were not immediately accommodated. It is now reported that Du Yuesheng of the Gold Exchange, Mu Ouchu of the Cotton Cloth Exchange, Wang Yiting of the Flour Exchange, and Gu Xinyi of the Grains Exchange, the chairmen of the four exchanges, jointly submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance for permission to postpone the tax. The original text is as follows: (Titles omitted) "We have examined the Transaction Tax Regulations, which were approved by the fourth meeting of the Legislative Yuan on February 8. This time, we are extremely grateful to the Ministry for understanding our difficulties and for being exceptionally accommodating in reducing the tax rates. However, since the opening of the market, the cotton cloth industry has not only continued the depression of last year, but has also become even more severe. Furthermore, due to the dumping of Japanese cotton mills in China, the business of Chinese cotton mills is deteriorating. Recently, the incident of Shenxin Factory No. 7 is sufficient to prove this point. It is difficult to predict the number of other factories that will follow Shenxin's footsteps. In the gold industry, business is sluggish due to the depression in the market and the decline in finance. We can only maintain the status quo. In flour, due to the dumping of foreign flour and the shrinkage of the domestic market (after the occupation of the four northeastern provinces, the domestic market has disappeared by more than half), sales are sluggish and business is greatly burdened. Although miscellaneous grains are a necessity for the lives of people across the country, the bankruptcy of rural areas and the recurrence of disasters, coupled with the competition from foreign grains, have made the plight of grain merchants even more precarious. Considering the situation of the above industries, we have repeatedly thought about it and have no choice but to reiterate our previous request for a postponement to save the current economic crisis. Moreover, a transaction tax was once announced in 1927, but it was not implemented due to our request at the time. The situation of the business community today is far worse than it was then. Furthermore, since Japan unilaterally advocated Sino-Japanese economic cooperation recently, Japan has been actively plotting activities in our economic circles, which is very aggressive. It is possible that the Japanese exchange will revive at any time. In order to maintain the sluggish business situation, it is necessary to postpone the transaction tax. Once the business situation improves in the future, the tax can be levied again, so that both the government and the business community can benefit. We humbly request that our request be granted, which would be a great kindness."

Revival of the Sichuan River Shipping Industry After Years of Failure 123

Financial Stability and Falling Exchange Rates; Plenty of Goods and Many Passengers, Each Increasing the Number of Runs; China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Is Discussing Adding Voyages

The Sichuan River shipping industry has been in decline for a long time. This time, after the Central Army entered Sichuan and defeated the Communists, commerce suddenly became prosperous and finance became stable, breaking the gloomy and dull atmosphere of the past few years. The recent report is as follows:

Smooth Financing

Last year, Sichuan merchants stopped handling goods because the Shanghai exchange rate rose to 1,700 yuan. The price of goods from Shanghai more than doubled. In addition, the interior of Sichuan was unstable, so various groups stopped shipping goods one after another, and the shipping industry suffered losses accordingly. Recently, the Central Government transported silver to Chongqing, the finance was liquid, and the exchange rate was flat. At present, it only costs 1,040 yuan to exchange one thousand Shanghai silver dollars in Sichuan. Therefore, various Sichuan merchants have recently telegraphed Shanghai, ordering the Shanghai dealers to handle the transportation of goods to Sichuan.

Crowding with Cargo, Increase in Voyages

The Communists who had been entrenched in Sichuan for many years have been defeated by the Central Army and the Sichuan Army. The bandit areas have been recovered one after another, and the requisitioned ships have been returned one after another. The water level of the Sichuan River has risen again, and Jianglun ships with a draft of eight or nine feet can pass through. Minsheng, Jiejang, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Sanbei have each increased the number of voyages of ships to Sichuan and Shanghai. The number of goods transported has increased greatly, and foreign groceries and cotton yarn are already being packed.

Great Increase in Passengers

Since Chairman Chiang arrived in Chongqing, the number of passengers traveling back and forth along the Sichuan River has doubled, which is many times more than in the past. As a result, demand exceeds supply. The passenger ticket income of the Sichuan River ships of Minsheng, Jiejang, and Sanbei has increased greatly, which is rare in the past 20 years of Sichuan River ships, breaking the previous record.

China Merchants Resumes Navigation

The Sichuan River ships of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company have not been sailing since the Emei ship accident. The Emei ship has not yet been repaired. There is only one Kuaidi ship in the Hanyi line. Last year, the total water foot was only more than 18,000 yuan (on the Upper River line), which is less than one-eighth of that of Taikoo and Jardine Matheson. Now is a good opportunity to revive the ships on the Upper River. The Yichang and Chongqing branches have telegraphed the Shanghai headquarters, requesting that Sichuan River ships be dispatched quickly to supplement the Emei class, so as not to sit idly by and abandon huge profits and lose good opportunities. Manager Liu Hongsheng is discussing adding voyages and resuming navigation on the Sichuan River.

Resolution of the Rent Reduction Problem in the Jiangwan District 124

All Paid at 60% or 70% Discount; the Rent Reduction Association Commends

Due to the economic downturn and business depression in Shanghai, all tenants in the city are unable to bear the burden of rent. Therefore, there was a great rent reduction movement last year. Recently, the Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee reported that the members of the Jiangwan District Association live in houses owned by 75 landlords, all of whom have reduced rents by 60% or 70%. The first branch of the district also requested 30 landlords to reduce rents, so a meeting of both parties was convened at the Jiangwan District Association the day before yesterday. As a result, the rent reduction was calculated at a 70% discount, so the rent reduction for each tenant was satisfactorily resolved. They have successively withdrawn the deposited rent money from the bank and paid the rent at a 70% discount. The Rent Reduction Association believes that the District Association has worked hard and should be commended.

Commemoration of the Birthday and Martyrdom of Song Jiaoren 125

Yu Youren Paid Respects at the Meeting Yesterday with Song's Son; Ju Zheng Telegraphed Tan Zhen Yesterday to Prepare Incense and Flowers for the Announcement

Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, accompanied Song Zhenlu, the son of the late martyr Song Jiaoren, left Beijing the night before last and took the 11:00 PM overnight express train to Shanghai, arriving in Shanghai at 7:20 AM yesterday morning. After getting off the train, he went straight to his private residence in Jing'an Villa to rest. Then, at 2:00 PM, he drove with Song's son and others to Song's tomb in Song Park Road, Zhabei, to pay respects, respectfully offering wreaths. According to those around Mr. Yu, Mr. Yu and Martyr Song were old friends during his lifetime, and today happens to be the birthday and memorial day of Mr. Song's martyrdom, so he came to pay respects. He will stay for a day or two and then return to Beijing. Mr. Yu's old illness has completely recovered. Tang Youren, Permanent Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs, Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and Liu Ruiheng, Director of the Department of Health, also arrived in Shanghai with Mr. Yu on the same train yesterday morning.

Nanjing telephone, Ju Zheng telegraphed Tan Zhen in Shanghai on the 22nd that the 28th is Song Jiaoren's birthday, "Mr. Song has passed away for 22 years. Looking at Song Park, we shed tears together. Today is the day of the new and old calendars of Mr. Dun's birthday and death anniversary. I sincerely hope that this opportunity can be used to sweep the tomb with him. Because of things that cannot be done, how sad! Please prepare incense and flowers for me and announce my name."

Treasury Department Public Debt Division Absolutely Denies Restructuring of the 96 Bonds 129

Because These Bonds Have No Collateral

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, recently, rumors have suddenly spread in the city that the financial authorities will begin to restructure the 96 public bonds. The rumors were very specific, causing public anxiety. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency drove to visit Jiang Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Division of the Treasury Department, yesterday afternoon to inquire about the matter. He was received and stated that this statement was completely a rumor spread by speculators and was absolutely untrue. Furthermore, these 96 public bonds were issued by the Northern Government and have no collateral at all. Moreover, given the current state of the national treasury, which is experiencing financial difficulties, there are many bonds that need to be restructured, so how could they talk about restructuring the 96 bonds? This matter is very clear. Several years ago, the people of North China twice requested the authorities to restructure the bonds, but the authorities refused each time because the bonds had absolutely no collateral. The matter has been delayed until now.

New Bridge Road Cracks Down on Counterfeit Coin Case Confiscates 1,220 Counterfeit Twenty-Cent Coins Court Hearing Yesterday Morning Ordered Further Investigation 130

Yang Peizhang, Jiang Juwu, and Wu Changkai, Chinese detectives of the New Bridge Police Station, and Bao Tai, a Western detective sergeant, successively cracked down on a case of counterfeiting in their jurisdiction the night before. The suspects, Chen Zhangrong, Wu Zhenxiang, Chen Wangshi, Zhang Wangshi, Shen Qianshi, and Shen Qinglin, were arrested. 1,220 counterfeit twenty-cent coins and counterfeiting equipment were confiscated and taken to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. Judge Liu Yugui presided over the interrogation. The police station charged them with the crime of counterfeiting under Article 211, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, then rose and detailed the circumstances of the case, stating that since the police station learned that the defendants were counterfeiting coins and mixing them into circulation, they had requested the court to issue a search warrant. At 6:05 PM yesterday, they first searched No. 5 Lao Street on New Bridge Road, where they arrested Chen Rongzhang, his wife Chen Wangshi, and Wu Zhenxiang. 127 counterfeit twenty-cent coins were confiscated, as well as 31 more found in their shoes, and two stamps with the characters "Ming" and "Shun." They then went to No. 189 Dong Siwen Lane, No. 568 New Bridge Road, where they arrested the woman Zhang Wangshi and confiscated 10 counterfeit twenty-cent coins. Subsequently, based on Wu Zhenxiang's confession that the counterfeiting workshop was located at No. 969 North Chengdu Road, the Chinese and Western detectives went there and arrested Shen Qianshi and Shen Qinglin. They confiscated 14 sets of manufacturing molds, a bottle of soldering acid, four dry batteries, and chemicals. They also found 1,052 counterfeit twenty-cent coins in a wooden box on the drying platform. All of these items were brought back to the police station. It was discovered that the counterfeiting workshop on North Chengdu Road was run by Shen Peisheng, who was at large. Shen is the husband of the defendant Shen Qianshi and hired Shen Qinglin as an assistant. They started working in January of this year and have produced a total of 2,500 coins so far. Their method of manufacturing involves first making a plaster mold of a genuine twenty-cent coin, then placing lead into the mold and pressing it into the shape of a twenty-cent coin. They then use chemicals and dry batteries to put the genuine silver coins and lead coins together, transferring the silver from the silver coins onto the lead coins. Wu Zhenxiang acted as an intermediary, selling the counterfeit coins to Chen Zhangrong for 8 yuan per 200 coins, and he sold them three times. Chen then added the Ming and Shun stamps and tried to use them in various small vegetable markets. Wu profited by receiving 10 cents each day. However, when police detectives went to the workshop on North Chengdu Road to arrest Shen Peisheng, Shen heard the alarm, hid the counterfeit coins in a wooden box on the drying platform, climbed onto the roof, and escaped, avoiding arrest. In addition, they confiscated opium smoking paraphernalia in all three locations and requested a ruling from the court. The confiscated items were then presented to the court. After Judge Liu interrogated the defendants, he ordered them to be remanded in custody because the case required further investigation and scheduled a hearing in seven days.

The defendant, Ding Chengfu, was brought in for questioning and stated that he is 23 years old, a local, graduated from higher primary school, and entered the Agricultural and Industrial Bank as a banknote clerk, where he has served for many years. This time, he was implicated by his colleagues and sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment. The judge asked if she disliked him for having legal troubles and did not want to marry him, and if he had any statement to make. Ding replied that he absolutely could not agree to dissolve the engagement. As for the legal troubles, he was harmed by friends and begged for completion of the marriage. The judge said that since she was unwilling, he could not force her. Moreover, when his sentence expires and he restores his reputation, it would not be difficult to get engaged again. He replied that he firmly disagreed. The questioning judge concluded that mediation had failed and instructed the petitioner to file a formal lawsuit separately. Ma Guanlin, a native of Ningbo, currently residing at No. 63 Guoqing Road, Zhabei, is 35 years old. In the early winter of last year, he and his friend Ge Xiangfu, among others, jointly established the Sanxing Steamship Company at the Dadao Wharf in Nanshi. Ge initially served as manager, and after chartering the Shunchang steamboat, he defrauded people of guarantee deposits for positions such as compradors and stewards. He originally agreed to settle with them. The plaintiffs then testified about their experiences of being defrauded, stating that all the guarantee deposits were handed over to Ma. The former manager, Ge Xiangfu, is also facing legal charges for fraud and is currently in prison. At this point, the judge instructed the defendant, stating that since he is a shareholder of the company, he should be responsible for repaying the money and cannot shirk responsibility. If he can settle the matter, the court will reschedule the hearing. He can present any other evidence at the next hearing. The judge also informed him that the hearing would be rescheduled for the 26th and ordered him to be returned to custody, fearing he might flee. The defendant's lawyer requested bail, but the court denied it. He then requested to be transferred to the detention center, which the court approved. The bailiffs then escorted the defendant to the detention center.

History of the Organization and Consolidation of China's Light Bulb Industry 143

A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Hu Xiyuan of the Ya Peier Electric Factory yesterday regarding the organization of China's Light Bulb Consolidation Company and inquired about the details. According to Mr. Hu, the initiation of China's Light Bulb Consolidation Company was in mid-November of last year. It was felt that various Chinese light bulb factories were acting independently in terms of business and manufacturing, with very little overall coordination. Therefore, the standards of products and methods of sales were not ideal. If manufacturers only seek short-term gains, producing shoddy goods and recklessly selling them on the market, it would damage the reputation of Chinese light bulbs as a whole. These weaknesses needed to be addressed, or else how could they compete with foreign light bulbs? Therefore, the motivation for organizing China's Light Bulb Consolidation Company was to develop strategies for trade against foreign goods. It was not for the benefit of one factory or for personal gain, but for the collective, not individual private interests. However, given that each factory has different capital and production, those who are restricted by the current environment and genuinely cannot participate will not be forced to agree. This plan is still actively underway. The members are determined to sacrifice their rights to promote its early realization.

Shanghai Municipal Council's Financial Situation 147

Surplus of 700,000 Taels Last Year; No Need to Increase Municipal Tax This Year

The Treasurer of the Shanghai Municipal Council reported to the Finance Committee that the budget for regular expenses last year, i.e., 1934, had a surplus of approximately 700,000 taels (previously it was predicted that there would only be a surplus of 40,000 taels). The various departments made great efforts to tighten their spending, resulting in total savings of approximately 1.1 million taels. However, tax revenues were also short by 430,000 taels, and the expenses of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee, 45,000 taels, were also not originally in the budget. But there was still a surplus as mentioned above.

As for the finances for this year, i.e., 1935, the regular expenses will require approximately 27.1 million taels, and the income is expected to be approximately 25.9 million taels, leaving a shortfall of approximately 1.2 million taels. The Treasurer stated that this would be paid from the general reserve fund. In this way, the municipal tax for this year can be exempted from increase.

Regarding the temporary budget, the bond issuance approved in the morning was not fully subscribed, and many of the land plots planned for sale were also not sold. Therefore, the year-end loss is expected to be 5.5 million taels, which will be included in the adjustments for this year. The construction costs for this year are lower than last year, mainly to complete projects that have already been started and unavoidable road work, along with debt repayment, as in the previous year.

The Treasurer stated that the current spending in all areas has been deferred to the extent possible. Once the financial situation in the city recovers to normal, the issuance of public bonds will be discussed again.

Letter 156

To the Editor: Having read the article in your newspaper on March 20th regarding the women's circles seeking peace, I yesterday telegraphed the Women's Disarmament Conference in Geneva, "The Chinese Women's Movement Alliance, during its March 8th meeting this year, had a proposal put forward by Zhou Jingjue and others, representatives of the Women's Branch of the Peace Association, requesting that the world's women telegraph the authorities of various countries, advocating for peace." According to the general rules of meetings, non-members have no right to make proposals. The statement "a proposal put forward by Zhou Jingjue and others, representatives of the Women's Branch of the Peace Association" is clearly inconsistent with the facts. Deeply fearing misunderstanding from the outside world, I hereby send a special letter, requesting that you correct it on our behalf. Wishing you peace, The Chinese Women's Movement Alliance, March 21st.

To Whom It May Concern: We are instructed by the Yongyu Shipping Company to state that, upon reading a news item in today's Shen Bao regarding the Chongming County detaining the Dalian ship for smuggling opium, it was stated that in January of this year, the police of the Chongming County Public Security Bureau found 1,000 packages of opium smuggled from Shanghai to Chongming in the Dalian ship's accounts room, and the county fined the shipowner, and now the old matter is being brought up again, and the county government, upon provincial order, has detained the ship and arrested the accountant, etc. It is found that the Dalian ship of this company was previously, in January, due to passengers privately carrying opium, which was seized by the police in the ship's steerage, and the criminals fled, which has no relation whatsoever to the Dalian ship. The claims of finding it in the accounts room and the shipowner being fined are without basis in fact. As for this time, it was falsely accused by someone from the Provincial Opium Prohibition Association, claiming that on the 3rd of this month, the Dasu ship smuggled a large amount of opium to Chongming for sale. The province, without investigating, hastily ordered the county to detain the Dasu ship. In reality, there was no seizure of opium on the 3rd of this month. This company cannot bear this slander and has already telegraphed the province for a thorough investigation and requested that the ship be released first to facilitate navigation. As for the Shen Bao's claim that this detention is a rehash of an old matter from January of this year, it is even further from the truth. It should be requested that your lawyer promptly issue a correction to clarify the situation, etc., which is hereby conveyed on behalf of the company. We hope you will investigate and correct it. Respectfully, To the Editorial Department of the Shen Bao, Lawyer Sun Zuji, March 22nd.

Special Announcement

Report on the Business of the Jin Cheng Bank for the Year 23 (10) 159

(2) Trade: Foreign trade in Soviet Russia is managed and operated under government control, and since 1932, import and export trade has shown a sharp downward trend. In 1929, the average monthly import value was 73.39 million rubles; in 1931, the monthly average rose to 92.09 million rubles; but in 1932, the monthly average import value suddenly decreased to 58.67 million rubles; in 1933, it further decreased to 29.02 million rubles. The total import value from January to September 1934 was 171.12 million rubles, averaging 19.01 million rubles per month, but most of these were tools for industrial production. Due to the sharp decrease in import trade, export trade also decreased accordingly. In 1929, the average monthly export value was 76.97 million rubles; in 1930, it increased to 86.36 million rubles; in 1931, it began to decrease to 67.6 million rubles; in 1932, it was 47.91 million rubles; in 1933, it further decreased to 41.31 million rubles. The total export value from January to September of this year (1934) was 302.03 million rubles, with the average monthly export value further decreasing to 33.56 million rubles. However, the decrease in Soviet Russia's export trade was weaker than that of import trade. Therefore, from 1930 to 1932, it was originally a country with an import surplus, but in 1933, it reversed from an import surplus to an export surplus, with an export surplus of 147.45 million rubles. The export surplus from January to September of this year (1934) was already 130.91 million rubles. Although we cannot see the whole picture, it is enough to see a glimpse of Soviet Russia's trade this year. (To be continued)

It is said that after the reorganization of the Chinese branch this time, participation from the literary and art circles is welcomed.

Postponement of Swearing-in Ceremony The Student National Goods Year Committee originally planned to hold the swearing-in ceremony at the Municipal Government on April 4th. Separate Celebrations The Children's Happiness Association originally intended to hold the Children's Day celebration jointly with the Student National Goods Year. However, since the association has rescheduled, it was decided to prepare independently. At the same time, as a large-scale opening ceremony for the Children's Year will be held on August 1st of this year, the current Children's Day will not be expanded to save money. Eight activity items for elementary schools during the current Children's Day have been drafted and submitted to the Municipal Education Bureau for implementation in schools. In addition, a recreational gathering and children's broadcasting session will be held at the Public Education Center on that day. The Shipping Radio Station will broadcast children's programs from 9:00 AM to 6:00 PM, with speeches by celebrities invited by the Children's Happiness Association.

Chen Heqin Returns from European Tour - Speaks on Education in England and Russia 177

The International Problems Research Association and the International Trade Association held a joint lecture meeting at the Bank Club the day before yesterday (the 20th), inviting Chen Heqin, Director of the Chinese Education Department of the Public Concession, to speak on "Impressions of a European Tour." Dozens of people, including Liu Zhanen, Huang Renzhi, Guo Bingwen, Li Zhaohuan, Chen Liting, Shen Xinqing, Cheng Haifeng, Zhang Xianglin, Xu Peihuang, and Chen Lingyi, attended. Liu Zhanen chaired the meeting. Mr. Chen spoke for an hour. The main points are summarized as follows: Heqin's trip to Europe to study education lasted seven months. Excluding the time spent on the ship, the actual investigation work was only five months. During these five months, he visited a total of eleven countries. The education in these eleven countries has its own characteristics. However, observing the education of many countries in a short period of time is inevitably a superficial experience. Here, I will focus on the more detailed observations of England and Russia.

England

(1) General Education: Since 1928, England has greatly reformed education. The curriculum and system have been transformed to meet modern needs. Children who are five years old must enter kindergarten, and at the age of seven, they enter primary school. From the ages of five to eleven, there are six years. After graduating from primary school, there are four avenues for further education after a rigorous examination: 1. Middle school; 2. Junior vocational school; 3. Central school; 4. Senior primary school. English middle schools still require tuition, but 20% of the places are free, reserved for poor but academically outstanding students. Middle schools are specifically for preparing for higher education. Those who are preparing for employment enter junior vocational schools after graduating from primary school. Those who are not preparing for higher education but wish to gain a slightly higher level of knowledge than primary school or to fulfill their compulsory education years enter central schools or senior primary schools. (2) Special Education: In addition to ordinary primary schools and kindergartens, special schools such as schools for the blind, deaf, and disabled are established in various cities. For children with intellectual disabilities, there are schools for children with intellectual disabilities to implement various special training programs. For children with lung diseases, there are also open-air classrooms for classes and recuperation. In short, all children in England, whether they are intelligent or foolish, healthy or disabled, have the opportunity to receive education. (3) Curriculum: In terms of curriculum, two aspects of English education are worth noting: A. Physical Education: Physical education is the most important aspect in the current English education system. The so-called "education of a gentlemanly demeanor" is mainly due to physical education. All primary and secondary schools pay attention to physical training. Various sports buildings and equipment are very common. In addition to public sports fields built by the government, each school has a gym. In Liverpool alone, there are more than ten privately built swimming pools that are open to the public, and each primary and secondary school also has a public swimming pool for students to practice. Swimming is a compulsory subject. Teachers lead students to swim on time every two weeks, regardless of wind, rain, cold, or heat. In the past, when teaching freehand exercises, students felt bored because they were done continuously from beginning to end of each class. Now, a mixed system has been adopted, in which exercises and games are taught alternately. For example, after ten minutes of exercise, a game is played, and then exercise is continued. As a result, students are very interested in exercise, and the efficiency of physical education classes has greatly increased. The physical condition of English children is exceptionally healthy. Looking back at Chinese children, we feel ashamed. B. Labor: The labor teaching materials in schools focus on practical training. Boys focus on handicrafts such as woodworking and metalworking. Girls' extracurricular activities focus on home economics, such as sewing, cooking, and laundry, all under the guidance of teachers. Children make their own clothes, cook snacks, and other practical items needed in daily life. The required expenses are entirely borne by the students themselves. If students are willing to sell their works, the school buys them at a reasonable price. The purpose of this type of education is to develop students' production skills so that they can support themselves in the future. This is the characteristic of labor education in England, and we should learn from it.

Russia

(1) Popular Education: Among European countries, Russia is a unique country. Their education is unique. We know that at the beginning of the Soviet revolution, their education was more immature and rudimentary than ours. However, the speed of recent educational progress is truly astonishing. There are a total of 150 different ethnic groups in the Soviet Union, each with its own different language or script. The situation is complex, as you can imagine. However, the Soviet government has achieved the goal of universal education in just thirteen years. There are now no illiterate citizens in the country, and seventy ethnic groups originally had no written language. Now, each has its own newly created written language. The majority of the people across the country, regardless of gender or age, read newspapers and books. The speed of educational progress is evident. (2) Children's Education: There are many school-age children in the Soviet Union. There are too few schools in each city to accommodate them. Therefore, the half-day system is temporarily adopted. Students are divided into morning and afternoon classes and attend and are taught in turns. Therefore, the capacity of the school is doubled, and the effectiveness of education is greatly increased. (3) Practice and Production: Russian schools have scientific research institutes and art research institutes. The scientific research institutes are further divided into departments such as telephone, machinery, radio, applied chemistry, aircraft, and automobiles. Children aged 11 to 17 choose a group with similar characteristics and practice research under the guidance of teachers. During my visit, I saw two cars, one large and one small, which were said to have been built by the students themselves. In short, the education in European countries can be said to be closely integrated with society. It is not pure book learning, but practical and realistic, not just a formality. This is what we should pay special attention to.

Special Article

German Science and Chinese Libraries (Part 1) 184

— By Dr. Jiejin, German Library Committee

Although the German scientific community and the Chinese academic community are separated by a great distance, the scientific ties between the two countries have not only been very close in recent years, but have also complemented each other. The number of Chinese youth studying in Germany is increasing year by year, and the number of German university professors lecturing at Chinese research institutions is also increasing year by year. German science has spread all over the world. In countries such as Turkey and South America, universities have been founded entirely in accordance with the German spirit and methods, and most of the professors hired by these universities are German. Chinese and German cultures have obvious similarities, and the starting point of pure scientific thought methods is completely the same. Based on this spirit, under close contact, the greatest effects can naturally continue to be harvested. China does not lack well-known figures who are proficient in German language, such as Zhu Jiahua, Minister of Transportation and former Minister of Education of the National Government, who was one of those who studied industry at German universities. This is a point that Germans are generally happy about. Germany has always strived for closer contact and has strived to fully utilize this contact in order to benefit both parties.

What is described in this article is not intended to describe the close contact between China and Germany in detail, but to simply explain a point that is easily overlooked by the general public. Although this point is not valued by people, it actually contains lasting and important significance. So, what is this? It is the relationship between German science and Chinese libraries. This article is based on the position of the German Academic Exchange Service.

The German Academic Exchange Service is the central organization for academic research in Germany. The Exchange Service's mission is to engage in scientific research and to establish relations with foreign countries in accordance with its regulations and will. Because it has already achieved good results in its own country, it will further establish a solid foundation for the Chinese knowledge community. It is necessary to thoroughly realize the ambition of making German libraries familiar with the Chinese situation, and in order to closely connect with the major Chinese libraries that pay attention to European literature and language, it has already received friendly responses from all parties in China in the process of mutual exchanges. China has a vast territory, and it is of course not within the scope of this article to describe the situation of contact in various aspects in detail. Therefore, what is described here is only a few of the most important institutions and the efforts made by the Exchange Service in this regard.

First of all, in Shanghai, at this time, 9,000 German books were donated by the Exchange Service and destroyed by Japanese soldiers. The Oriental Library, which is now being rebuilt, is receiving this batch of books, which have already been sent from Germany to China. In order to facilitate readers to enjoy the important books of the New Germany, this collection contains monographs on various aspects of the past and present struggles of the Germans. This kind of book is attached with magnificent myths and stories and has the latest factory building images. Another part describes German cooperative societies, which are the only well-equipped in Europe and are models for the whole of Europe. Many people come to Germany every year to visit this facility. This type of book also has illustrations. Even readers with a shallow level of German can easily get a glimpse of where the German spirit is and where the great German culture lies after opening the book. Another part is about German law. This type of book can be regarded as the standard of modern law books. As for other aspects, only representative works are collected. These works are all produced under the assistance of the Exchange Service, rare scientific experiments, and are collected for the convenience of Chinese experts. As for some older versions of the books, they are all donated by scientific tycoons and libraries. From this type of book, we can know that the Exchange Service also accepts both old and new books. It is hoped that readers will learn from the past and know the new. This is the purpose of including old books. There is also a part of German poetry. Chinese people who love poetry may be able to better understand the essence of Germany by reading this.

Washing off the rouge on the lips and cheeks of all the fashionable women in the country might turn the Yellow Sea into the Red Sea: scraping off the powder on their faces might be enough to paint a twenty-two-story building: taking off the high heels of their leather shoes and connecting them one by one might be higher than the pyramids.

Mid-Spring Season 186

— Qifenglou Master

The call for spring has reached the world, and people have been shouting for it for a long time. Spring is the most lovely season of the year, because everything about it gives people pleasure and love, which of course can win the warm welcome of the masses! Although the earth is calling for the return of spring, the cold is still strong. Everyone is calling for the chilling spring cold, which is still a pity. By the time of late spring in March, the grass grows and the warblers fly, and it will leave without any reluctance, only increasing the infinite melancholy of those who grieve for spring! This beautiful nature really makes people intoxicated!

"A year's plan lies in spring" This is known to everyone, but how many people can work hard in the spring? Now spring is half gone. In the blink of an eye, the water flows, the flowers fall, and the spring is old. Where can you buy youth with gold! Although the god of spring is smiling gently at the masses, it is disciplined and knows to move forward bravely! Never hesitating for a moment! Moreover, for the sake of meaningless things, they have abandoned the important mission of life and done the dead end of suicide and self-destruction. This is too much to live up to the great spring, right?

The Whale's Doomsday 187

— Kangjianzhaifu

Whales, in the ocean, have always had the majestic image of being "invincible in the world." But in this day and age, it seems to have become "a turtle in a jar."

In the past, the tools for whaling were unfavorable, and the methods of hunting whales were still considered to be open warfare. Whales had many opportunities to escape. Since the advent of the bombing-style harpoon, the method of assassination has been used, and the behemoth has had no choice but to surrender. It is said that the exploding harpoon weighs one hundred and twenty pounds and contains twenty-eight pounds of explosives. In general, whales weighing about eighty tons to one hundred tons are inevitably killed by one touch.

At present, the whales in the Arctic Ocean have almost been captured by Norwegian fishermen. There are twenty whaling ships in the Antarctic Ocean, and usually there are one hundred and fifty small whaling fishing boats. It is expected that before the summer of this year, 30,000 whales can be invited by them to land for sightseeing and be slaughtered by the whale factory. There are as many as six thousand Norwegians acting as executioners of whales in the Antarctic Ocean. Unless the whaling fleet considers the virtue of the heavens to love life and gives them a way out, all the whales in the world will be in danger of their offspring disappearing within a few years. The vast sea has no place for it to live!

Prehistoric large animals, such as dinosaurs, have long been extinct in the world. The existing large animals, whales can be regarded as second to none. If it really follows the dinosaurs and disappears soon, it can be regarded as a deeply regrettable event in the history of biology. But who taught you to contain such enviable fat in yourself, and not have a bit of the ability to resist and defend yourself!

The Philosophy of Matches 188

— Liu Baishe

Matches, this object, in Beiping is called "qudeng" (fire-getter), in Shanghai "zilaihuo" (self-igniting fire), in Jiangbei "yanghuo" (foreign fire), in Japan "rinsun" (phosphorus inch), in the West "match," though the names differ, the thing is the same. Since the "fire steel" was abandoned, matches have become a necessity for every household, a thing everyone uses, and thus striking matches has become something everyone does, and the philosophy of matches is thus invented! Observing the postures and habits of various people when striking matches with a cold eye, one can know their intelligence, foolishness, virtue, treachery... Generally, those who strike inwards are often meticulous, those who strike outwards are often careless, those who rub a long portion are surely foolish, those who rub a short portion are surely clever, those who strike two or three at once must not be economical, those who strike one and use it for two or more guests must be good at socializing, those who casually discard the ashes on the ground must be romantic or lazy, those who forcefully throw away the ashes must be decisive and brave, those who blow out the ashes must be leisurely and slow, those who slowly watch the ashes burn out must be sinister and have deep intentions, those who talk to others and take an unlit match, carelessly breaking it into several pieces and playing with it, must be cunning and scheming. Judging people in this way, how can anyone hide? How can anyone conceal themselves? If you don't believe me, please try it.

Astonishing Numbers! 190

— (Jiaoxin)

It is said that in Jiangsu Province alone, the monthly consumption of opium is 1,200 dan (a unit of weight), which is 14,400 dan per year. With each tael valued at 2.5 yuan, the money consumed in the tiny holes of those tea-bean-sized opium pipes each year is 57,600,000 yuan! How can the nation not be poor! How can the people not be weak!

However, this is only Jiangsu Province. If we were to calculate the total consumption of the entire country, it would truly make your jaw drop!

Records of the Fragrant Imperial Aroma 191

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

After the cocoons are taken from the silkworms, the most cruel scene appears! Regardless of whether the pupae live or die, they throw the cocoons into boiling water, alive, killing the silkworm pupae. After the cocoons have soaked in boiling water for a few moments, they are constantly stirred with a short bamboo tool until a silk thread can be drawn from one of the cocoons. Then they stop stirring, first attaching the thread to a thin cocoon. When the thread is finished, they attach the thread of the second cocoon and continue stirring. In this way, they can obtain skeins of raw silk. I watched the girls doing this with interest and volunteered to try it for a while, but I couldn't draw out a single thread. Of course, this kind of work requires considerable learning! From this point of view, silk workers can be considered a kind of artisan with specialized skills. However, I don't envy them. I just feel that the existence of silkworms is truly the most interesting thing, so I want to study it thoroughly.

"Old Buddha, there's still something I don't understand," I asked Empress Dowager Cixi while she was in a good mood, "Now that these cocoons have been boiled, where will we get silkworms next year?"

"There's no need to worry about that! We have already selected a portion of the cocoons specifically for breeding." She explained patiently, "The pupae inside the cocoons will change! As long as we don't scald them to death, after a certain period, they will turn into silkworm moths. These silkworm moths will never stay in the cocoons again. They will automatically bite a small hole in the cocoons and crawl out. Sometimes, the girls who raise silkworms will even help them tear the cocoons to let them out sooner..." (275)

World Wonders

Sleeping Beauty 192

— Qing Qu

Previously, this newspaper reported from the China United Press in Chicago that a Western woman named Miss McGirr, 29 years old, fainted on February 15, 1932, while putting on her coat to go out. She fell onto the bed and has been asleep ever since, without waking for thirty-three months, and is known as Sleeping Beauty. Even many doctors do not know what ails her. This year, in January, her mother, Mrs. Milly, discovered that her daughter could open her eyes, and was overjoyed. She wrote words with a pen to show her, and indeed, she recognized them without error. Therefore, the news spread far and wide, saying that there is hope for a cure for the long-sleeping illness. I, for my part, believe that sleeping and becoming ill, and that the illness should be so deep and prolonged, is not unique to Miss McGirr. Let me describe a few examples, so that the reader may be informed.

The reason why people want to sleep is mainly due to mental exhaustion, so overwork leads to fatigue, and fatigue leads to weariness. Secondly, it is loneliness, and thirdly, it is stomach discomfort, or else it is a normal state. All animals have the reason to sleep, fish in the water, even if they are extremely lively, cannot rest. Sleep has a length and shortness, therefore waking also has a difficulty. During deep sleep, even the noise of gongs and drums cannot be heard, while during a light doze, even the sound of footsteps outside the door can be identified by the person. This is the depth of sleep, and awakening is tied to it. To sleep is to be named an illness, then it is not exhaustion, loneliness, or stomach discomfort, but it is also different from the normal state. In the past, a noblewoman in France suffered from this illness from 1883, lasting for sixteen years. She was on the verge of death, almost paralyzed, appearing dead at first glance, but not really dead. Every second she still had eighty heartbeats, but shaking her, her face was blank and unaware. Giving her food, she drank a little broth; not giving her anything, she did not ask for it. After medical treatment, it was said that the body's capillaries are innumerable; if they are relaxed, one is awake; if they are closed, one is asleep. This woman's capillaries were constantly closed and not relaxed, so she constantly slept and did not wake up. The saying has a lot of insight, but it cannot be definitively concluded.

In the land of Geena in Africa, there were scholars in the past who suffered from this sleeping sickness, lying in bed for four years, always associated with pillows, and their mouths were constantly closed, no longer needing food and drink. Some called them "living immortals." Their families used milk, cheese, and other things, injecting them into their stomachs through nasal tubes to prolong their remaining breath. Later, doctors invented "life-saving devices" to test them. The person's sleep was like the person's death. When this device was placed on the chest, if there was even a slight breath, the device would move accordingly, allowing one to see if they were alive or dead, even if they were indeed dead. It was necessary to examine them before people embalmed them, which shows how serious the sleeping sickness can be. This time, Miss McGirr slept for two years and nine months. After this long period of black and sweet dream life, her mother suddenly saw her eyeballs able to move, and took paper and pen to write words, saying "Raise one finger," and the girl slowly responded. Then she wrote "Raise two fingers," and the girl responded again, without any error. From this it was known that she was awake, no longer a person in a dream. But this still cannot be without doubt, let us use one saying to clarify it.

If a person stares at a child, or a weak person, if they directly face their eyes, their expression can immediately change to dazed, and they lose their subjectivity. If, at this time, you tell them that you are in the mountains, then the person suddenly feels like they are on a cliff. If you tell them that you are in the water, then the person is like they are in the sea. If you give them something bitter and say it is sweet, then it is truly sweet. If you give them something hard and say it is soft, then it is truly soft. The five senses and four limbs can all be placed in a passive position. People only know hypnosis, but they can also awaken. Therefore, whether Miss McGirr's temporary awakening was induced by her mother's psychology is also a question. Therefore, I briefly describe it to provide assistance to those who can research this disease.

Chapter Eleven: Nighttime Conversation, A Bleak Life is But a Dream, Scattered Footprints, The Wind and Rain Are Too Oppressive

Generally speaking, whether a person is successful or unsuccessful, the expression of true feelings is most likely to gain the sympathy of others.
